Overall design:


A large, Victorian-style mansion with three stories
Main structure built primarily with red bricks
Steep black roof made of dark wood or wool
White trim and accents throughout the exterior


Exterior features:


Asymmetrical layout with a prominent central tower
Multiple gabled roofs at different heights
Large windows with white frames, some arched at the top
Decorative white quartz or concrete trim around windows, doors, and corners
White pillars supporting a small porch at the entrance
Ivy or vines growing on some parts of the walls


Roof details:


Steep black roofs made of dark oak stairs or black wool
White trim along the edges of the roof
Small dormer windows on some roof sections
Decorative chimneys made of brick and stone


Landscaping:


Surrounded by a lush garden with various flowers and plants
Custom trees made with oak logs and leaves
Grass blocks as the base, with coarse dirt and podzol for texture
Stone and gravel paths leading to the entrance and around the garden
Small pond or water feature near the house
Wooden fences and gates defining garden areas


Garden features:


Raised flower beds using wooden planks or stone bricks
Small greenhouse structure made of glass and wood
Garden benches and tables made from stairs and slabs
Lanterns or glowstone for exterior lighting
Beehives and bee nests in some tree branches


Entrance area:


Grand staircase leading to the front door
Small covered porch with white pillars
Wooden double doors as the main entrance


Additional exterior details:


Balconies on upper floors with white fences or railings
Bay windows on some parts of the house
Hanging lanterns or chain decorations


Interior (visible through windows):


High ceilings with chandeliers
Wooden flooring (oak or spruce planks)
Large windows allowing natural light
Visible wooden beams on the ceiling
Fireplaces made of brick and stone


Color scheme:


Red bricks for main walls
White quartz or concrete for trim and accents
Black wool or dark oak for the roof
Various colors for flowers and garden elements

Ensure the structure has a grand, imposing feel with intricate details and a well-maintained garden. The house should appear elegant and slightly whimsical, befitting a Victorian-era mansion in a Minecraft world.
